## Migration Steps

### Step 1: Setup Directory Structure

```bash
# Create main directories
mkdir -p /volume1/docker/{nginx,pocketbase}

# Create nginx subdirectories
mkdir -p /volume1/docker/nginx/{configs/sites-available,configs/ssl,scripts}

# Create pocketbase subdirectories  
mkdir -p /volume1/docker/pocketbase/{data/{pb_data,pb_public,pb_migrations},scripts}

# Set proper ownership for pocketbase data
chown -R 1028:100 /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/
```

### Step 2: Deploy Configuration Files

```bash
# Copy all the config files shown above to their respective locations
# nginx.conf -> /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/nginx.conf
# site configs -> /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/
```

### Step 3: Deploy Single Stack in Portainer

1. **Deploy the combined stack:**
   - Go to Stacks in Portainer
   - Create new stack: `web-apps`
   - Paste the updated compose content (includes both nginx and pocketbase)
   - Deploy

### Step 4: Test New Setup

- Visit `http://mind.eatonfamily.net` (should work via your reverse proxy)
- Visit `http://calcium.eatonfamily.net`  
- Visit `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-dev/`
- Visit `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/calcium-dev/`
- Check PocketBase admin: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-dev/_/`

### Step 5: Migrate PocketBase Data (After Testing)

Once the new containers are working:
```bash
# Stop the new stack temporarily
# Copy data from old location to new
cp -r /volume1/projects/mind-pwa/pocketbase/pb_data/* /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_data/
cp -r /volume1/projects/mind-pwa/pocketbase/pb_public/* /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_public/
cp -r /volume1/projects/mind-pwa/pocketbase/pb_migrations/* /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_migrations/

# Fix ownership
chown -R 1028:100 /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/

# Restart stack in Portainer
```

## Management Scripts

### Environment-Aware Nginx Reload Script

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/scripts/reload-config.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash
echo "🔄 Testing nginx configuration..."
if docker exec nginx-proxy nginx -t; then
    echo "✅ Configuration is valid, reloading..."
    docker exec nginx-proxy nginx -s reload
    echo "✅ Configuration reloaded successfully"
    echo ""
    echo "🌐 Available endpoints:"
    echo "  Production:"
    echo "    - https://mind.eatonfamily.net"
    echo "    - https://calcium.eatonfamily.net"
    echo "  Development (Local):"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/Ca-pwa-dev/"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/_/ (PocketBase Admin)"
else
    echo "❌ Configuration test failed! Not reloading."
    exit 1
fi
```

### Utility Scripts - When and How to Use

The migration plan includes several utility scripts. Here's when you'd use each:

#### **1. `reload-config.sh` - Most Common**
**When to use:**
- After making changes to nginx configuration files
- After adding new sites or modifying existing ones
- When troubleshooting nginx issues

**How to use:**
```bash
cd /volume1/docker/nginx/scripts
./reload-config.sh
```

**Why it's useful:**
- Tests configuration before applying (prevents breaking nginx)
- Shows you all available endpoints after reload
- Safer than restarting the entire container

#### **2. `add-site.sh` - When Adding New Apps**
**When to use:**
- Adding a brand new web application
- Setting up staging environments for existing apps

**How to use:**
```bash
cd /volume1/docker/nginx/scripts
./add-site.sh myapp myapp.eatonfamily.net
```

**What it does:**
- Creates nginx config template for new app
- Tells you what volume mount to add in Portainer
- Provides both static and PocketBase-enabled templates

#### **3. PocketBase Scripts (Future)**
These would be useful for data management:

**`/volume1/docker/pocketbase/scripts/backup.sh`** - Database backups
**`/volume1/docker/pocketbase/scripts/restore.sh`** - Database restoration

### Script Usage Frequency

**Daily Development:**
- Your existing deployment scripts: `./deploy.sh dev/prod`
- No utility scripts needed

**Weekly/Monthly:**
- `reload-config.sh` - When adding features or new apps
- Your scripts handle 99% of routine work

**Rarely (New Apps):**
- `add-site.sh` - Only when adding completely new applications
- Backup/restore scripts - Only for major changes or migrations

### Your Scripts Are Excellent

Your deployment scripts are actually **better** than the utility scripts for routine work because they:
- ✅ Handle the full build-deploy cycle
- ✅ Support multiple environments seamlessly  
- ✅ Include error handling and validation
- ✅ Show build sizes and helpful output
- ✅ Are specific to your app needs

The utility scripts are more for **infrastructure changes** rather than **application deployments**.

## Benefits of This Architecture

### Add New Site Template

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/scripts/add-site.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash
SITE_NAME=$1
DOMAIN=$2

if [ -z "$SITE_NAME" ] || [ -z "$DOMAIN" ]; then
    echo "Usage: $0 <site-name> <domain>"
    echo "Example: $0 todoapp todo.eatonfamily.net"
    exit 1
fi

cat > "/volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/${DOMAIN}.conf" << EOF
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name ${DOMAIN};

    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data:;" always;

    location / {
        root /usr/share/nginx/html/${SITE_NAME};
        try_files \$uri \$uri/ /index.html;
        
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|woff|woff2)\$ {
            expires 1y;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        location = /index.html {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # Uncomment if app needs PocketBase backend:
    # location /api/ {
    #     proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
    #     proxy_set_header Host \$host;
    #     proxy_set_header X-Real-IP \$remote_addr;
    #     proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For \$proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
    #     proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto \$scheme;
    #     proxy_http_version 1.1;
    #     proxy_set_header Upgrade \$http_upgrade;
    #     proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
    # }
}
EOF

echo "✅ Created config for ${DOMAIN}"
echo "📝 Remember to:"
echo "   1. Add volume mount in Portainer: /volume1/web/${SITE_NAME}-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/${SITE_NAME}:ro"
echo "   2. Restart nginx-proxy stack"
```

With this configuration, your development URLs will be (matching your current setup):
- **MIND Diet Tracker Dev**: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/`
- **Calcium Tracker Dev**: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/Ca-pwa-dev/`
- **PocketBase Admin**: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/_/`

### Your Deployment Scripts Work Perfectly!

Looking at your deployment scripts, they're excellent and **no changes needed**:

✅ **MIND App Scripts:**
- `./deploy-client.sh dev` → deploys to `/volume1/web/mind-pwa-dev`
- `./deploy-pocketbase.sh dev` → deploys to `/volume1/web/mind-pwa-dev` 

✅ **Calcium App Script:**
- `./deploy.sh dev` → deploys to `/volume1/web/Ca-pwa-dev`
- `./deploy.sh prod` → deploys to `/volume1/web/Ca-pwa-deploy`

### Development Workflow (No Changes Required)
```bash
# Deploy MIND app for development
cd /volume1/projects/mind-pwa
./deploy-pocketbase.sh dev
# Visit: http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/

# Deploy Calcium app for development  
cd /volume1/projects/Ca-pwa
./deploy.sh dev
# Visit: http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/Ca-pwa-dev/

# Deploy to production when ready
./deploy-pocketbase.sh prod  # MIND
./deploy.sh prod            # Calcium
```

1. **Modular**: Nginx and PocketBase are separate, manageable stacks
2. **Scalable**: Easy to add new apps without complex reconfigurations  
3. **Maintainable**: All configurations are version-controlled and organized
4. **Flexible**: Apps can use PocketBase or be purely static
5. **Production Ready**: Proper security, caching, and health checks
6. **Portainer Friendly**: Managed through familiar UI with proper dependency handling

## Future Expansion

When you add new apps:
1. Deploy app static files to `/volume1/web/newapp-deploy`
2. Run `add-site.sh newapp newapp.eatonfamily.net`
3. Update nginx-proxy stack to include new volume mount
4. Apps automatically get shared PocketBase access if needed

This setup gives you a robust foundation for your development work while being production-ready!

<file path="configs/sites-available/calcium-dev.eatonfamily.net.conf">
# Development/Staging environment for Calcium Tracker
server {
    # Nginx container listens on port 80. Your NAS reverse proxy handles the 443 -> 8080 -> 80 forwarding.
    listen 80;
    
    # This server block will be used for requests to this specific domain.
    server_name calcium-dev.eatonfamily.net;

    # Security header to allow connections to your Cloudflare Worker for sync.
    # This is important for the sync functionality to work.
    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; connect-src 'self' https://*.workers.dev; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data:;" always;

    # This handles all requests for this domain.
    location / {
        # The root path for this site, inside the Docker container.
        # This matches the volume mapping in your docker-compose.yml for the dev environment.
        root /usr/share/nginx/html/Ca-pwa-dev;

        # Standard SPA (Single-Page App) fallback rule.
        # This ensures that deep links like /stats or /data are handled by the app's router.
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;

        # Development-friendly caching rules to ensure you always see the latest changes.
        add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
    }
}
</file>

<file path="configs/sites-available/calcium.eatonfamily.net.conf">
# Production Calcium Tracker
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name calcium.eatonfamily.net;

    # Standard security for static app
    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data:;" always;

    # Static files only
    location / {
        root /usr/share/nginx/html/calcium;
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;
        
        # Cache static assets
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|woff|woff2)$ {
            expires 1y;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        # Don't cache HTML files
        location = /index.html {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # Future: If calcium app needs PocketBase, add API routes here
    # location /api/ {
    #     proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
    #     # ... same proxy config as mind app
    # }
}
</file>

<file path="configs/sites-available/local-dev.conf">
# Add this to your nginx configuration for local development access
# This should go in /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/local-dev.conf

# Local development server block
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name eatonmediasvr.local;

    # MIND App Development
    location /mind-pwa-dev/ {
        alias /usr/share/nginx/html/mind-pwa-dev/;
        try_files $uri $uri/ /mind-pwa-dev/index.html;
        
        # Minimal caching for development
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|woff|woff2)$ {
            expires 5m;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        # No caching for HTML files in dev
        location ~* \.html$ {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # PocketBase API for MIND dev
    location /mind-pwa-dev/api/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
        proxy_http_version 1.1;
        proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;
        proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
    }

    # PocketBase Admin for MIND dev
    location /mind-pwa-dev/_/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/_/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
    }

    # Calcium App Development
    location /Ca-pwa-dev/ {
        # Point to the PARENT directory. Nginx will append the location path.
        root /usr/share/nginx/html;

        # The SPA fallback rule. This is the most important part.
        # It tries to find the file directly, and if it fails, serves the index.html
        # from within the app's own subdirectory.
        try_files $uri $uri/ /Ca-pwa-dev/index.html;

        # Your caching rules for assets and HTML can live here,
        # but for simplicity and to ensure it works, let's start without them.
        # You can add the nested location blocks for caching back in *after*
        # you confirm the routing works.
        add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
    }

    # Root location for server info or redirect
    location = / {
        return 200 "Development Server - Available apps: /mind-pwa-dev/, /Ca-pwa-dev/";
        add_header Content-Type text/plain;
    }

    # Health check
    location /health {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/health;
        access_log off;
    }
}
</file>

<file path="configs/sites-available/mind.eatonfamily.net.conf">
# Production MIND Diet Tracker
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name mind.eatonfamily.net;

    # Enhanced security for app with backend
    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data:; connect-src 'self';" always;

    # Static files
    location / {
        root /usr/share/nginx/html/mind;
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;
        
        # Cache static assets
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|woff|woff2)$ {
            expires 1y;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        # Don't cache HTML files
        location = /index.html {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # PocketBase API
    location /api/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
        proxy_http_version 1.1;
        proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;
        proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
    }

    # PocketBase Admin (development access)
    location /_/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/_/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
    }

    # Health check
    location /health {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/health;
        access_log off;
    }
}

<file path="configs/nginx.conf">
user nginx;
worker_processes auto;
error_log /var/log/nginx/error.log notice;
pid /var/run/nginx.pid;

events {
    worker_connections 1024;
}

http {
    include /etc/nginx/mime.types;
    default_type application/octet-stream;

    # Logging
    log_format main '$remote_addr - $remote_user [$time_local] "$request" '
                    '$status $body_bytes_sent "$http_referer" '
                    '"$http_user_agent" "$http_x_forwarded_for"';
    access_log /var/log/nginx/access.log main;

    # Performance
    sendfile on;
    tcp_nopush on;
    keepalive_timeout 65;
    gzip on;
    gzip_vary on;
    gzip_min_length 1024;
    gzip_types text/plain text/css text/xml text/javascript application/javascript application/xml+rss application/json;

    # Security headers (default)
    add_header X-Frame-Options DENY always;
    add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff always;
    add_header X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block" always;
    add_header Referrer-Policy "strict-origin-when-cross-origin" always;

    # PocketBase upstream (shared across all apps)
    upstream pocketbase_backend {
        server pocketbase-backend:8090;
    }

    # Include site-specific configurations
    include /etc/nginx/sites-available/*.conf;
}
</file>

<file path="scripts/reload-config.sh">
#!/bin/bash
echo "🔄 Testing nginx configuration..."
if docker exec nginx-proxy nginx -t; then
    echo "✅ Configuration is valid, reloading..."
    docker exec nginx-proxy nginx -s reload
    echo "✅ Configuration reloaded successfully"
    echo ""
    echo "🌐 Available endpoints:"
    echo "  Production:"
    echo "    - https://mind.eatonfamily.net"
    echo "    - https://calcium.eatonfamily.net"
    echo "  Development (Local):"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/Ca-pwa-dev/"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/_/ (PocketBase Admin)"
else
    echo "❌ Configuration test failed! Not reloading."
    exit 1
fi

<file path="docker-compose.yml">
version: '3.8'

services:
  nginx:
    image: nginx:latest
    container_name: nginx-proxy
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "8080:80"  # Match your working config - reverse proxy handles 443->8080
    volumes:
      # Configuration
      - /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
      - /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available:/etc/nginx/sites-available:ro
      - /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/ssl:/etc/nginx/ssl:ro
      # Production static content
      - /volume1/web/mind-pwa-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/mind:ro
      - /volume1/web/Ca-pwa-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/calcium:ro
      # Development static content (matches your current paths)
      - /volume1/web/mind-pwa-dev:/usr/share/nginx/html/mind-pwa-dev:ro
      - /volume1/web/Ca-pwa-dev:/usr/share/nginx/html/Ca-pwa-dev:ro
    environment:
      - NGINX_ENVSUBST_TEMPLATE_SUFFIX=.template
    networks:
      - web-proxy
    depends_on:
      - pocketbase
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "nginx", "-t"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

  pocketbase:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile_inline: |
        FROM alpine:latest
        RUN apk add --no-cache curl unzip ca-certificates wget
        WORKDIR /pb
        # Use fixed version to avoid variable expansion issues
        RUN curl -L "https://github.com/pocketbase/pocketbase/releases/download/v0.28.1/pocketbase_0.28.1_linux_amd64.zip" -o pb.zip \
            && unzip pb.zip \
            && rm pb.zip \
            && chmod +x pocketbase
        VOLUME /pb_data
        EXPOSE 8090
        CMD ["./pocketbase", "serve", "--http=0.0.0.0:8090"]
    container_name: pocketbase-backend
    restart: unless-stopped
    user: "1028:100"
    expose:
      - "8090"
    volumes:
      # Keep separate from existing data for now - migrate later
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_data:/pb/pb_data
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_public:/pb/pb_public
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_migrations:/pb/pb_migrations
    environment:
      - PB_DATA_DIR=/pb/pb_data
      - PB_PUBLIC_DIR=/pb/pb_public
      - PB_MIGRATIONS_DIR=/pb/pb_migrations
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "wget", "--quiet", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:8090/api/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    networks:
      - web-proxy

networks:
  web-proxy:
    driver: bridge
</file>

<file path="README.md">
# Production Migration Plan: Nginx + PocketBase Multi-App Infrastructure

## Revised Architecture Overview

**Goal:** Create a scalable, general-purpose web app infrastructure using:
- **Nginx**: General reverse proxy for all web apps (not just nutrition apps)
- **PocketBase**: Multi-tenant backend supporting multiple apps with shared user accounts
- **Portainer**: Container management via stacks
- **Modular Design**: Easy to add new apps without nginx reconfiguration headaches

## Directory Structure

```
/volume1/docker/
├── nginx/
│   ├── docker-compose.yml
│   ├── configs/
│   │   ├── nginx.conf
│   │   ├── sites-available/
│   │   │   ├── mind.eatonfamily.net.conf
│   │   │   ├── calcium.eatonfamily.net.conf
│   │   │   └── default.conf
│   │   └── ssl/ (for future certificates)
│   └── scripts/
│       ├── reload-config.sh
│       └── add-site.sh
├── pocketbase/
│   ├── docker-compose.yml
│   ├── configs/
│   │   └── Dockerfile
│   ├── data/
│   │   ├── pb_data/
│   │   ├── pb_public/
│   │   └── pb_migrations/
│   └── scripts/
│       ├── backup.sh
│       └── restore.sh
```

## Portainer Stack Configurations

### Stack 1: Nginx (General Web Proxy)

**Stack Name:** `nginx-proxy`  
**Compose file for Portainer:**

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  nginx:
    image: nginx:latest
    container_name: nginx-proxy
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "80:80"
      # Remove 443 for now - add back later when you're ready for SSL
      # - "443:443"
    volumes:
      # Configuration
      - /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
      - /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available:/etc/nginx/sites-available:ro
      - /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/ssl:/etc/nginx/ssl:ro
      # Production static content
      - /volume1/web/mind-pwa-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/mind:ro
      - /volume1/web/Ca-pwa-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/calcium:ro
      # Development static content (matches your current paths)
      - /volume1/web/mind-pwa-dev:/usr/share/nginx/html/mind-pwa-dev:ro
      - /volume1/web/Ca-pwa-dev:/usr/share/nginx/html/Ca-pwa-dev:ro
      # Future apps can be added here
      # - /volume1/web/otherapp-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/otherapp:ro
      # - /volume1/web/otherapp-dev:/usr/share/nginx/html/otherapp-dev:ro
    environment:
      - NGINX_ENVSUBST_TEMPLATE_SUFFIX=.template
    networks:
      - web-proxy
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "nginx", "-t"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

networks:
  web-proxy:
    external: true
```

### Stack 2: PocketBase (Multi-App Backend)

**Stack Name:** `pocketbase-backend`  

**Option A: Using Pre-built Image (Recommended for Portainer)**
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  pocketbase:
    image: ghcr.io/muchobien/pocketbase:latest
    container_name: pocketbase-backend
    restart: unless-stopped
    user: "1028:100"
    expose:
      - "8090"
    volumes:
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_data:/pb_data
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_public:/pb_public
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_migrations:/pb_migrations
    environment:
      - POCKETBASE_DATA_DIR=/pb_data
      - POCKETBASE_PUBLIC_DIR=/pb_public
      - POCKETBASE_MIGRATIONS_DIR=/pb_migrations
    command: ["serve", "--http=0.0.0.0:8090"]
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "wget", "--quiet", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:8090/api/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    networks:
      - web-proxy
      - pocketbase-internal

networks:
  web-proxy:
    external: true
  pocketbase-internal:
    driver: bridge
```

**Option B: If you prefer building from your Dockerfile**
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  pocketbase:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile_inline: |
        FROM alpine:latest
        RUN apk add --no-cache curl unzip ca-certificates wget
        WORKDIR /pb
        ENV PB_VERSION=0.28.1
        RUN curl -L "https://github.com/pocketbase/pocketbase/releases/download/v${PB_VERSION}/pocketbase_${PB_VERSION}_linux_amd64.zip" -o pb.zip \
            && unzip pb.zip \
            && rm pb.zip \
            && chmod +x pocketbase
        VOLUME /pb_data
        EXPOSE 8090
        CMD ["./pocketbase", "serve", "--http=0.0.0.0:8090", "--publicDir=/pb/pb_public"]
    container_name: pocketbase-backend
    restart: unless-stopped
    user: "1028:100"
    expose:
      - "8090"
    volumes:
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_data:/pb/pb_data
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_public:/pb/pb_public
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_migrations:/pb/pb_migrations
    environment:
      - PB_DATA_DIR=/pb/pb_data
      - PB_PUBLIC_DIR=/pb/pb_public
      - PB_MIGRATIONS_DIR=/pb/pb_migrations
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "wget", "--quiet", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:8090/api/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    networks:
      - web-proxy
      - pocketbase-internal

networks:
  web-proxy:
    external: true
  pocketbase-internal:
    driver: bridge
```

## Configuration Files

### Main Nginx Configuration

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/configs/nginx.conf`

```nginx
user nginx;
worker_processes auto;
error_log /var/log/nginx/error.log notice;
pid /var/run/nginx.pid;

events {
    worker_connections 1024;
}

http {
    include /etc/nginx/mime.types;
    default_type application/octet-stream;

    # Logging
    log_format main '$remote_addr - $remote_user [$time_local] "$request" '
                    '$status $body_bytes_sent "$http_referer" '
                    '"$http_user_agent" "$http_x_forwarded_for"';
    access_log /var/log/nginx/access.log main;

    # Performance
    sendfile on;
    tcp_nopush on;
    keepalive_timeout 65;
    gzip on;
    gzip_vary on;
    gzip_min_length 1024;
    gzip_types text/plain text/css text/xml text/javascript application/javascript application/xml+rss application/json;

    # Security headers (default)
    add_header X-Frame-Options DENY always;
    add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff always;
    add_header X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block" always;
    add_header Referrer-Policy "strict-origin-when-cross-origin" always;

    # PocketBase upstream (shared across all apps)
    upstream pocketbase_backend {
        server pocketbase-backend:8090;
    }

    # Include site-specific configurations
    include /etc/nginx/sites-available/*.conf;
}
```

### MIND Diet Tracker Site Configs

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/mind.eatonfamily.net.conf`

```nginx
# Production MIND Diet Tracker
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name mind.eatonfamily.net;

    # Enhanced security for app with backend
    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data:; connect-src 'self';" always;

    # Static files
    location / {
        root /usr/share/nginx/html/mind;
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;
        
        # Cache static assets
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|woff|woff2)$ {
            expires 1y;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        # Don't cache HTML files
        location = /index.html {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # PocketBase API
    location /api/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
        proxy_http_version 1.1;
        proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;
        proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
    }

    # PocketBase Admin (development access)
    location /_/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/_/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
    }

    # Health check
    location /health {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/health;
        access_log off;
    }
}

# Development MIND Diet Tracker
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name mind-dev.eatonfamily.net;

    # Relaxed caching for development
    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data:; connect-src 'self';" always;

    # Static files from dev deployment
    location / {
        root /usr/share/nginx/html/mind-dev;
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;
        
        # Minimal caching for development
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|woff|woff2)$ {
            expires 5m;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        # No caching for HTML files in dev
        location = /index.html {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # Same PocketBase API (shared backend)
    location /api/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
        proxy_http_version 1.1;
        proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;
        proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
    }

    # PocketBase Admin
    location /_/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/_/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
    }

    # Health check
    location /health {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/health;
        access_log off;
    }
}
```

### Default/Catch-all Site Config

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/default.conf`

```nginx

server {
    listen 80 default_server;
    server_name _;
    
    # Return 444 (close connection) for unmatched domains
    return 444;
}

## Migration Steps

### Step 1: Setup Directory Structure

```bash
# Create main directories
mkdir -p /volume1/docker/{nginx,pocketbase}

# Create nginx subdirectories
mkdir -p /volume1/docker/nginx/{configs/sites-available,configs/ssl,scripts}

# Create pocketbase subdirectories  
mkdir -p /volume1/docker/pocketbase/{data/{pb_data,pb_public,pb_migrations},scripts}

# Set proper ownership for pocketbase data
chown -R 1028:100 /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/
```

### Step 2: Deploy Configuration Files

```bash
# Copy all the config files shown above to their respective locations
# nginx.conf -> /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/nginx.conf
# site configs -> /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/
```

### Step 3: Deploy Single Stack in Portainer

1. **Deploy the combined stack:**
   - Go to Stacks in Portainer
   - Create new stack: `web-apps`
   - Paste the updated compose content (includes both nginx and pocketbase)
   - Deploy

### Step 4: Test New Setup

- Visit `http://mind.eatonfamily.net` (should work via your reverse proxy)
- Visit `http://calcium.eatonfamily.net`  
- Visit `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-dev/`
- Visit `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/calcium-dev/`
- Check PocketBase admin: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-dev/_/`

### Step 5: Migrate PocketBase Data (After Testing)

Once the new containers are working:
```bash
# Stop the new stack temporarily
# Copy data from old location to new
cp -r /volume1/projects/mind-pwa/pocketbase/pb_data/* /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_data/
cp -r /volume1/projects/mind-pwa/pocketbase/pb_public/* /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_public/
cp -r /volume1/projects/mind-pwa/pocketbase/pb_migrations/* /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_migrations/

# Fix ownership
chown -R 1028:100 /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/

# Restart stack in Portainer
```

## Management Scripts

### Environment-Aware Nginx Reload Script

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/scripts/reload-config.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash
echo "🔄 Testing nginx configuration..."
if docker exec nginx-proxy nginx -t; then
    echo "✅ Configuration is valid, reloading..."
    docker exec nginx-proxy nginx -s reload
    echo "✅ Configuration reloaded successfully"
    echo ""
    echo "🌐 Available endpoints:"
    echo "  Production:"
    echo "    - https://mind.eatonfamily.net"
    echo "    - https://calcium.eatonfamily.net"
    echo "  Development (Local):"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/Ca-pwa-dev/"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/_/ (PocketBase Admin)"
else
    echo "❌ Configuration test failed! Not reloading."
    exit 1
fi
```

### Utility Scripts - When and How to Use

The migration plan includes several utility scripts. Here's when you'd use each:

#### **1. `reload-config.sh` - Most Common**
**When to use:**
- After making changes to nginx configuration files
- After adding new sites or modifying existing ones
- When troubleshooting nginx issues

**How to use:**
```bash
cd /volume1/docker/nginx/scripts
./reload-config.sh
```

**Why it's useful:**
- Tests configuration before applying (prevents breaking nginx)
- Shows you all available endpoints after reload
- Safer than restarting the entire container

#### **2. `add-site.sh` - When Adding New Apps**
**When to use:**
- Adding a brand new web application
- Setting up staging environments for existing apps

**How to use:**
```bash
cd /volume1/docker/nginx/scripts
./add-site.sh myapp myapp.eatonfamily.net
```

**What it does:**
- Creates nginx config template for new app
- Tells you what volume mount to add in Portainer
- Provides both static and PocketBase-enabled templates

#### **3. PocketBase Scripts (Future)**
These would be useful for data management:

**`/volume1/docker/pocketbase/scripts/backup.sh`** - Database backups
**`/volume1/docker/pocketbase/scripts/restore.sh`** - Database restoration

### Script Usage Frequency

**Daily Development:**
- Your existing deployment scripts: `./deploy.sh dev/prod`
- No utility scripts needed

**Weekly/Monthly:**
- `reload-config.sh` - When adding features or new apps
- Your scripts handle 99% of routine work

**Rarely (New Apps):**
- `add-site.sh` - Only when adding completely new applications
- Backup/restore scripts - Only for major changes or migrations

### Your Scripts Are Excellent

Your deployment scripts are actually **better** than the utility scripts for routine work because they:
- ✅ Handle the full build-deploy cycle
- ✅ Support multiple environments seamlessly  
- ✅ Include error handling and validation
- ✅ Show build sizes and helpful output
- ✅ Are specific to your app needs

The utility scripts are more for **infrastructure changes** rather than **application deployments**.

## Benefits of This Architecture

### Add New Site Template

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/scripts/add-site.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash
SITE_NAME=$1
DOMAIN=$2

if [ -z "$SITE_NAME" ] || [ -z "$DOMAIN" ]; then
    echo "Usage: $0 <site-name> <domain>"
    echo "Example: $0 todoapp todo.eatonfamily.net"
    exit 1
fi

cat > "/volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/${DOMAIN}.conf" << EOF
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name ${DOMAIN};

    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data:;" always;

    location / {
        root /usr/share/nginx/html/${SITE_NAME};
        try_files \$uri \$uri/ /index.html;
        
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|woff|woff2)\$ {
            expires 1y;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        location = /index.html {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # Uncomment if app needs PocketBase backend:
    # location /api/ {
    #     proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
    #     proxy_set_header Host \$host;
    #     proxy_set_header X-Real-IP \$remote_addr;
    #     proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For \$proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
    #     proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto \$scheme;
    #     proxy_http_version 1.1;
    #     proxy_set_header Upgrade \$http_upgrade;
    #     proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
    # }
}
EOF

echo "✅ Created config for ${DOMAIN}"
echo "📝 Remember to:"
echo "   1. Add volume mount in Portainer: /volume1/web/${SITE_NAME}-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/${SITE_NAME}:ro"
echo "   2. Restart nginx-proxy stack"
```

## Additional Considerations for Dev/Prod Setup

### Local Development URLs
With this configuration, your development URLs will be (matching your current setup):
- **MIND Diet Tracker Dev**: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/`
- **Calcium Tracker Dev**: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/Ca-pwa-dev/`
- **PocketBase Admin**: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/_/`

### Your Deployment Scripts Work Perfectly!

Looking at your deployment scripts, they're excellent and **no changes needed**:

✅ **MIND App Scripts:**
- `./deploy-client.sh dev` → deploys to `/volume1/web/mind-pwa-dev`
- `./deploy-pocketbase.sh dev` → deploys to `/volume1/web/mind-pwa-dev` 

✅ **Calcium App Script:**
- `./deploy.sh dev` → deploys to `/volume1/web/Ca-pwa-dev`
- `./deploy.sh prod` → deploys to `/volume1/web/Ca-pwa-deploy`

### Development Workflow (No Changes Required)
```bash
# Deploy MIND app for development
cd /volume1/projects/mind-pwa
./deploy-pocketbase.sh dev
# Visit: http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/

# Deploy Calcium app for development  
cd /volume1/projects/Ca-pwa
./deploy.sh dev
# Visit: http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/Ca-pwa-dev/

# Deploy to production when ready
./deploy-pocketbase.sh prod  # MIND
./deploy.sh prod            # Calcium
```

1. **Modular**: Nginx and PocketBase are separate, manageable stacks
2. **Scalable**: Easy to add new apps without complex reconfigurations  
3. **Maintainable**: All configurations are version-controlled and organized
4. **Flexible**: Apps can use PocketBase or be purely static
5. **Production Ready**: Proper security, caching, and health checks
6. **Portainer Friendly**: Managed through familiar UI with proper dependency handling

## Future Expansion

When you add new apps:
1. Deploy app static files to `/volume1/web/newapp-deploy`
2. Run `add-site.sh newapp newapp.eatonfamily.net`
3. Update nginx-proxy stack to include new volume mount
4. Apps automatically get shared PocketBase access if needed

This setup gives you a robust foundation for your development work while being production-ready!

# Production Migration Plan: Nginx + PocketBase Multi-App Infrastructure

## Revised Architecture Overview

**Goal:** Create a scalable, general-purpose web app infrastructure using:
- **Nginx**: General reverse proxy for all web apps (not just nutrition apps)
- **PocketBase**: Multi-tenant backend supporting multiple apps with shared user accounts
- **Portainer**: Container management via stacks
- **Modular Design**: Easy to add new apps without nginx reconfiguration headaches

## Directory Structure

```
/volume1/docker/
├── nginx/
│   ├── docker-compose.yml
│   ├── configs/
│   │   ├── nginx.conf
│   │   ├── sites-available/
│   │   │   ├── mind.eatonfamily.net.conf
│   │   │   ├── calcium.eatonfamily.net.conf
│   │   │   └── default.conf
│   │   └── ssl/ (for future certificates)
│   └── scripts/
│       ├── reload-config.sh
│       └── add-site.sh
├── pocketbase/
│   ├── docker-compose.yml
│   ├── configs/
│   │   └── Dockerfile
│   ├── data/
│   │   ├── pb_data/
│   │   ├── pb_public/
│   │   └── pb_migrations/
│   └── scripts/
│       ├── backup.sh
│       └── restore.sh
```

## Portainer Stack Configurations

### Stack 1: Nginx (General Web Proxy)

**Stack Name:** `nginx-proxy`  
**Compose file for Portainer:**

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  nginx:
    image: nginx:latest
    container_name: nginx-proxy
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "80:80"
      # Remove 443 for now - add back later when you're ready for SSL
      # - "443:443"
    volumes:
      # Configuration
      - /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
      - /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available:/etc/nginx/sites-available:ro
      - /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/ssl:/etc/nginx/ssl:ro
      # Production static content
      - /volume1/web/mind-pwa-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/mind:ro
      - /volume1/web/Ca-pwa-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/calcium:ro
      # Development static content (matches your current paths)
      - /volume1/web/mind-pwa-dev:/usr/share/nginx/html/mind-pwa-dev:ro
      - /volume1/web/Ca-pwa-dev:/usr/share/nginx/html/Ca-pwa-dev:ro
      # Future apps can be added here
      # - /volume1/web/otherapp-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/otherapp:ro
      # - /volume1/web/otherapp-dev:/usr/share/nginx/html/otherapp-dev:ro
    environment:
      - NGINX_ENVSUBST_TEMPLATE_SUFFIX=.template
    networks:
      - web-proxy
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "nginx", "-t"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

networks:
  web-proxy:
    external: true
```

### Stack 2: PocketBase (Multi-App Backend)

**Stack Name:** `pocketbase-backend`  

**Option A: Using Pre-built Image (Recommended for Portainer)**
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  pocketbase:
    image: ghcr.io/muchobien/pocketbase:latest
    container_name: pocketbase-backend
    restart: unless-stopped
    user: "1028:100"
    expose:
      - "8090"
    volumes:
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_data:/pb_data
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_public:/pb_public
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_migrations:/pb_migrations
    environment:
      - POCKETBASE_DATA_DIR=/pb_data
      - POCKETBASE_PUBLIC_DIR=/pb_public
      - POCKETBASE_MIGRATIONS_DIR=/pb_migrations
    command: ["serve", "--http=0.0.0.0:8090"]
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "wget", "--quiet", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:8090/api/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    networks:
      - web-proxy
      - pocketbase-internal

networks:
  web-proxy:
    external: true
  pocketbase-internal:
    driver: bridge
```

**Option B: If you prefer building from your Dockerfile**
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  pocketbase:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile_inline: |
        FROM alpine:latest
        RUN apk add --no-cache curl unzip ca-certificates wget
        WORKDIR /pb
        ENV PB_VERSION=0.28.1
        RUN curl -L "https://github.com/pocketbase/pocketbase/releases/download/v${PB_VERSION}/pocketbase_${PB_VERSION}_linux_amd64.zip" -o pb.zip \
            && unzip pb.zip \
            && rm pb.zip \
            && chmod +x pocketbase
        VOLUME /pb_data
        EXPOSE 8090
        CMD ["./pocketbase", "serve", "--http=0.0.0.0:8090", "--publicDir=/pb/pb_public"]
    container_name: pocketbase-backend
    restart: unless-stopped
    user: "1028:100"
    expose:
      - "8090"
    volumes:
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_data:/pb/pb_data
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_public:/pb/pb_public
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_migrations:/pb/pb_migrations
    environment:
      - PB_DATA_DIR=/pb/pb_data
      - PB_PUBLIC_DIR=/pb/pb_public
      - PB_MIGRATIONS_DIR=/pb/pb_migrations
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "wget", "--quiet", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:8090/api/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    networks:
      - web-proxy
      - pocketbase-internal

networks:
  web-proxy:
    external: true
  pocketbase-internal:
    driver: bridge
```

## Configuration Files

### Main Nginx Configuration

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/configs/nginx.conf`

```nginx
user nginx;
worker_processes auto;
error_log /var/log/nginx/error.log notice;
pid /var/run/nginx.pid;

events {
    worker_connections 1024;
}

http {
    include /etc/nginx/mime.types;
    default_type application/octet-stream;

    # Logging
    log_format main '$remote_addr - $remote_user [$time_local] "$request" '
                    '$status $body_bytes_sent "$http_referer" '
                    '"$http_user_agent" "$http_x_forwarded_for"';
    access_log /var/log/nginx/access.log main;

    # Performance
    sendfile on;
    tcp_nopush on;
    keepalive_timeout 65;
    gzip on;
    gzip_vary on;
    gzip_min_length 1024;
    gzip_types text/plain text/css text/xml text/javascript application/javascript application/xml+rss application/json;

    # Security headers (default)
    add_header X-Frame-Options DENY always;
    add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff always;
    add_header X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block" always;
    add_header Referrer-Policy "strict-origin-when-cross-origin" always;

    # PocketBase upstream (shared across all apps)
    upstream pocketbase_backend {
        server pocketbase-backend:8090;
    }

    # Include site-specific configurations
    include /etc/nginx/sites-available/*.conf;
}
```

### MIND Diet Tracker Site Configs

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/mind.eatonfamily.net.conf`

```nginx
# Production MIND Diet Tracker
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name mind.eatonfamily.net;

    # Enhanced security for app with backend
    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data:; connect-src 'self';" always;

    # Static files
    location / {
        root /usr/share/nginx/html/mind;
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;
        
        # Cache static assets
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|woff|woff2)$ {
            expires 1y;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        # Don't cache HTML files
        location = /index.html {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # PocketBase API
    location /api/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
        proxy_http_version 1.1;
        proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;
        proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
    }

    # PocketBase Admin (development access)
    location /_/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/_/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
    }

    # Health check
    location /health {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/health;
        access_log off;
    }
}

# Development MIND Diet Tracker
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name mind-dev.eatonfamily.net;

    # Relaxed caching for development
    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data:; connect-src 'self';" always;

    # Static files from dev deployment
    location / {
        root /usr/share/nginx/html/mind-dev;
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;
        
        # Minimal caching for development
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|woff|woff2)$ {
            expires 5m;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        # No caching for HTML files in dev
        location = /index.html {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # Same PocketBase API (shared backend)
    location /api/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
        proxy_http_version 1.1;
        proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;
        proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
    }

    # PocketBase Admin
    location /_/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/_/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
    }

    # Health check
    location /health {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/health;
        access_log off;
    }
}
```

### Calcium Tracker Site Configs

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/calcium.eatonfamily.net.conf`

# Production Calcium Tracker
server {

    # Static files only

        # Cache static assets

            expires 1y;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        # Don't cache HTML files
        location = /index.html {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # Future: If calcium app needs PocketBase, add API routes here
    # location /api/ {
    #     proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
    #     # ... same proxy config as mind app
    # }
}
```

### Default/Catch-all Site Config

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/default.conf`

```nginx
# Default server block (catch-all)
server {
    listen 80 default_server;
    server_name _;
    
    # Return 444 (close connection) for unmatched domains
    return 444;
}

# Future production apps can be added as separate .conf files:
#

#     server_name newapp.eatonfamily.net;
#     
#     location / {
#         root /usr/share/nginx/html/newapp;
#         try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;
#     }
#     
#     # Add /api/ block if app needs PocketBase
# }
```

## Migration Steps

### Step 1: Setup Directory Structure

```bash
# Create main directories
mkdir -p /volume1/docker/{nginx,pocketbase}

# Create nginx subdirectories
mkdir -p /volume1/docker/nginx/{configs/sites-available,configs/ssl,scripts}

# Create pocketbase subdirectories  
mkdir -p /volume1/docker/pocketbase/{data/{pb_data,pb_public,pb_migrations},scripts}

# Set proper ownership for pocketbase data
chown -R 1028:100 /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/
```

### Step 2: Deploy Configuration Files

```bash
# Copy all the config files shown above to their respective locations
# nginx.conf -> /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/nginx.conf
# site configs -> /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/
```

### Step 3: Deploy Single Stack in Portainer

1. **Deploy the combined stack:**
   - Go to Stacks in Portainer
   - Create new stack: `web-apps`
   - Paste the updated compose content (includes both nginx and pocketbase)
   - Deploy

### Step 4: Test New Setup

- Visit `http://mind.eatonfamily.net` (should work via your reverse proxy)
- Visit `http://calcium.eatonfamily.net`  
- Visit `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-dev/`
- Visit `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/calcium-dev/`
- Check PocketBase admin: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-dev/_/`

### Step 5: Migrate PocketBase Data (After Testing)

Once the new containers are working:
```bash
# Stop the new stack temporarily
# Copy data from old location to new
cp -r /volume1/projects/mind-pwa/pocketbase/pb_data/* /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_data/
cp -r /volume1/projects/mind-pwa/pocketbase/pb_public/* /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_public/
cp -r /volume1/projects/mind-pwa/pocketbase/pb_migrations/* /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_migrations/

# Fix ownership
chown -R 1028:100 /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/

# Restart stack in Portainer
```

## Management Scripts

### Environment-Aware Nginx Reload Script

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/scripts/reload-config.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash
echo "🔄 Testing nginx configuration..."
if docker exec nginx-proxy nginx -t; then
    echo "✅ Configuration is valid, reloading..."
    docker exec nginx-proxy nginx -s reload
    echo "✅ Configuration reloaded successfully"
    echo ""
    echo "🌐 Available endpoints:"
    echo "  Production:"
    echo "    - https://mind.eatonfamily.net"
    echo "    - https://calcium.eatonfamily.net"
    echo "  Development (Local):"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/Ca-pwa-dev/"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/_/ (PocketBase Admin)"
else
    echo "❌ Configuration test failed! Not reloading."
    exit 1
fi
```

### Utility Scripts - When and How to Use

The migration plan includes several utility scripts. Here's when you'd use each:

#### **1. `reload-config.sh` - Most Common**
**When to use:**
- After making changes to nginx configuration files
- After adding new sites or modifying existing ones
- When troubleshooting nginx issues

**How to use:**
```bash
cd /volume1/docker/nginx/scripts
./reload-config.sh
```

**Why it's useful:**
- Tests configuration before applying (prevents breaking nginx)
- Shows you all available endpoints after reload
- Safer than restarting the entire container

#### **2. `add-site.sh` - When Adding New Apps**
**When to use:**
- Adding a brand new web application
- Setting up staging environments for existing apps

**How to use:**
```bash
cd /volume1/docker/nginx/scripts
./add-site.sh myapp myapp.eatonfamily.net
```

**What it does:**
- Creates nginx config template for new app
- Tells you what volume mount to add in Portainer
- Provides both static and PocketBase-enabled templates

#### **3. PocketBase Scripts (Future)**
These would be useful for data management:

**`/volume1/docker/pocketbase/scripts/backup.sh`** - Database backups
**`/volume1/docker/pocketbase/scripts/restore.sh`** - Database restoration

### Script Usage Frequency

**Daily Development:**
- Your existing deployment scripts: `./deploy.sh dev/prod`
- No utility scripts needed

**Weekly/Monthly:**
- `reload-config.sh` - When adding features or new apps
- Your scripts handle 99% of routine work

**Rarely (New Apps):**
- `add-site.sh` - Only when adding completely new applications
- Backup/restore scripts - Only for major changes or migrations

### Your Scripts Are Excellent

Your deployment scripts are actually **better** than the utility scripts for routine work because they:
- ✅ Handle the full build-deploy cycle
- ✅ Support multiple environments seamlessly  
- ✅ Include error handling and validation
- ✅ Show build sizes and helpful output
- ✅ Are specific to your app needs

The utility scripts are more for **infrastructure changes** rather than **application deployments**.

## Benefits of This Architecture

### Add New Site Template

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/scripts/add-site.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash
SITE_NAME=$1
DOMAIN=$2

if [ -z "$SITE_NAME" ] || [ -z "$DOMAIN" ]; then
    echo "Usage: $0 <site-name> <domain>"
    echo "Example: $0 todoapp todo.eatonfamily.net"
    exit 1
fi

cat > "/volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/${DOMAIN}.conf" << EOF
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name ${DOMAIN};

    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data:;" always;

    location / {
        root /usr/share/nginx/html/${SITE_NAME};
        try_files \$uri \$uri/ /index.html;
        
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|woff|woff2)\$ {
            expires 1y;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        location = /index.html {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # Uncomment if app needs PocketBase backend:
    # location /api/ {
    #     proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
    #     proxy_set_header Host \$host;
    #     proxy_set_header X-Real-IP \$remote_addr;
    #     proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For \$proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
    #     proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto \$scheme;
    #     proxy_http_version 1.1;
    #     proxy_set_header Upgrade \$http_upgrade;
    #     proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
    # }
}
EOF

echo "✅ Created config for ${DOMAIN}"
echo "📝 Remember to:"
echo "   1. Add volume mount in Portainer: /volume1/web/${SITE_NAME}-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/${SITE_NAME}:ro"
echo "   2. Restart nginx-proxy stack"
```

## Additional Considerations for Dev/Prod Setup

### Local Development URLs
With this configuration, your development URLs will be (matching your current setup):
- **MIND Diet Tracker Dev**: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/`
- **Calcium Tracker Dev**: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/Ca-pwa-dev/`
- **PocketBase Admin**: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/_/`

### Your Deployment Scripts Work Perfectly!

Looking at your deployment scripts, they're excellent and **no changes needed**:

✅ **MIND App Scripts:**
- `./deploy-client.sh dev` → deploys to `/volume1/web/mind-pwa-dev`
- `./deploy-pocketbase.sh dev` → deploys to `/volume1/web/mind-pwa-dev` 

✅ **Calcium App Script:**
- `./deploy.sh dev` → deploys to `/volume1/web/Ca-pwa-dev`
- `./deploy.sh prod` → deploys to `/volume1/web/Ca-pwa-deploy`

### Development Workflow (No Changes Required)
```bash
# Deploy MIND app for development
cd /volume1/projects/mind-pwa
./deploy-pocketbase.sh dev
# Visit: http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/

# Deploy Calcium app for development  
cd /volume1/projects/Ca-pwa
./deploy.sh dev
# Visit: http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/Ca-pwa-dev/

# Deploy to production when ready
./deploy-pocketbase.sh prod  # MIND
./deploy.sh prod            # Calcium
```

1. **Modular**: Nginx and PocketBase are separate, manageable stacks
2. **Scalable**: Easy to add new apps without complex reconfigurations  
3. **Maintainable**: All configurations are version-controlled and organized
4. **Flexible**: Apps can use PocketBase or be purely static
5. **Production Ready**: Proper security, caching, and health checks
6. **Portainer Friendly**: Managed through familiar UI with proper dependency handling

## Future Expansion

When you add new apps:
1. Deploy app static files to `/volume1/web/newapp-deploy`
2. Run `add-site.sh newapp newapp.eatonfamily.net`
3. Update nginx-proxy stack to include new volume mount
4. Apps automatically get shared PocketBase access if needed

This setup gives you a robust foundation for your development work while being production-ready!

# Production Migration Plan: Nginx + PocketBase Multi-App Infrastructure

## Revised Architecture Overview

**Goal:** Create a scalable, general-purpose web app infrastructure using:
- **Nginx**: General reverse proxy for all web apps (not just nutrition apps)
- **PocketBase**: Multi-tenant backend supporting multiple apps with shared user accounts
- **Portainer**: Container management via stacks
- **Modular Design**: Easy to add new apps without nginx reconfiguration headaches

## Directory Structure

```
/volume1/docker/
├── nginx/
│   ├── docker-compose.yml
│   ├── configs/
│   │   ├── nginx.conf
│   │   ├── sites-available/
│   │   │   ├── mind.eatonfamily.net.conf
│   │   │   ├── calcium.eatonfamily.net.conf
│   │   │   └── default.conf
│   │   └── ssl/ (for future certificates)
│   └── scripts/
│       ├── reload-config.sh
│       └── add-site.sh
├── pocketbase/
│   ├── docker-compose.yml
│   ├── configs/
│   │   └── Dockerfile
│   ├── data/
│   │   ├── pb_data/
│   │   ├── pb_public/
│   │   └── pb_migrations/
│   └── scripts/
│       ├── backup.sh
│       └── restore.sh
```

## Portainer Stack Configurations

### Stack 1: Nginx (General Web Proxy)

**Stack Name:** `nginx-proxy`  
**Compose file for Portainer:**

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  nginx:
    image: nginx:latest
    container_name: nginx-proxy
    restart: unless-stopped
    ports:
      - "80:80"
      # Remove 443 for now - add back later when you're ready for SSL
      # - "443:443"
    volumes:
      # Configuration
      - /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf:ro
      - /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available:/etc/nginx/sites-available:ro
      - /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/ssl:/etc/nginx/ssl:ro
      # Production static content
      - /volume1/web/mind-pwa-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/mind:ro
      - /volume1/web/Ca-pwa-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/calcium:ro
      # Development static content (matches your current paths)
      - /volume1/web/mind-pwa-dev:/usr/share/nginx/html/mind-pwa-dev:ro
      - /volume1/web/Ca-pwa-dev:/usr/share/nginx/html/Ca-pwa-dev:ro
      # Future apps can be added here
      # - /volume1/web/otherapp-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/otherapp:ro
      # - /volume1/web/otherapp-dev:/usr/share/nginx/html/otherapp-dev:ro
    environment:
      - NGINX_ENVSUBST_TEMPLATE_SUFFIX=.template
    networks:
      - web-proxy
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "nginx", "-t"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3

networks:
  web-proxy:
    external: true
```

### Stack 2: PocketBase (Multi-App Backend)

**Stack Name:** `pocketbase-backend`  

**Option A: Using Pre-built Image (Recommended for Portainer)**
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  pocketbase:
    image: ghcr.io/muchobien/pocketbase:latest
    container_name: pocketbase-backend
    restart: unless-stopped
    user: "1028:100"
    expose:
      - "8090"
    volumes:
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_data:/pb_data
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_public:/pb_public
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_migrations:/pb_migrations
    environment:
      - POCKETBASE_DATA_DIR=/pb_data
      - POCKETBASE_PUBLIC_DIR=/pb_public
      - POCKETBASE_MIGRATIONS_DIR=/pb_migrations
    command: ["serve", "--http=0.0.0.0:8090"]
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "wget", "--quiet", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:8090/api/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    networks:
      - web-proxy
      - pocketbase-internal

networks:
  web-proxy:
    external: true
  pocketbase-internal:
    driver: bridge
```

**Option B: If you prefer building from your Dockerfile**
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  pocketbase:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile_inline: |
        FROM alpine:latest
        RUN apk add --no-cache curl unzip ca-certificates wget
        WORKDIR /pb
        ENV PB_VERSION=0.28.1
        RUN curl -L "https://github.com/pocketbase/pocketbase/releases/download/v${PB_VERSION}/pocketbase_${PB_VERSION}_linux_amd64.zip" -o pb.zip \
            && unzip pb.zip \
            && rm pb.zip \
            && chmod +x pocketbase
        VOLUME /pb_data
        EXPOSE 8090
        CMD ["./pocketbase", "serve", "--http=0.0.0.0:8090", "--publicDir=/pb/pb_public"]
    container_name: pocketbase-backend
    restart: unless-stopped
    user: "1028:100"
    expose:
      - "8090"
    volumes:
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_data:/pb/pb_data
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_public:/pb/pb_public
      - /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_migrations:/pb/pb_migrations
    environment:
      - PB_DATA_DIR=/pb/pb_data
      - PB_PUBLIC_DIR=/pb/pb_public
      - PB_MIGRATIONS_DIR=/pb/pb_migrations
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "wget", "--quiet", "--tries=1", "--spider", "http://localhost:8090/api/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 3
      start_period: 40s
    networks:
      - web-proxy
      - pocketbase-internal

networks:
  web-proxy:
    external: true
  pocketbase-internal:
    driver: bridge
```

## Configuration Files

### Main Nginx Configuration

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/configs/nginx.conf`

```nginx
user nginx;
worker_processes auto;
error_log /var/log/nginx/error.log notice;
pid /var/run/nginx.pid;

events {
    worker_connections 1024;
}

http {
    include /etc/nginx/mime.types;
    default_type application/octet-stream;

    # Logging
    log_format main '$remote_addr - $remote_user [$time_local] "$request" '
                    '$status $body_bytes_sent "$http_referer" '
                    '"$http_user_agent" "$http_x_forwarded_for"';
    access_log /var/log/nginx/access.log main;

    # Performance
    sendfile on;
    tcp_nopush on;
    keepalive_timeout 65;
    gzip on;
    gzip_vary on;
    gzip_min_length 1024;
    gzip_types text/plain text/css text/xml text/javascript application/javascript application/xml+rss application/json;

    # Security headers (default)
    add_header X-Frame-Options DENY always;
    add_header X-Content-Type-Options nosniff always;
    add_header X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block" always;
    add_header Referrer-Policy "strict-origin-when-cross-origin" always;

    # PocketBase upstream (shared across all apps)
    upstream pocketbase_backend {
        server pocketbase-backend:8090;
    }

    # Include site-specific configurations
    include /etc/nginx/sites-available/*.conf;
}
```

### MIND Diet Tracker Site Configs

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/mind.eatonfamily.net.conf`

```nginx
# Production MIND Diet Tracker
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name mind.eatonfamily.net;

    # Enhanced security for app with backend
    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data:; connect-src 'self';" always;

    # Static files
    location / {
        root /usr/share/nginx/html/mind;
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;
        
        # Cache static assets
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|woff|woff2)$ {
            expires 1y;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        # Don't cache HTML files
        location = /index.html {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # PocketBase API
    location /api/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
        proxy_http_version 1.1;
        proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;
        proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
    }

    # PocketBase Admin (development access)
    location /_/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/_/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
    }

    # Health check
    location /health {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/health;
        access_log off;
    }
}

# Development MIND Diet Tracker
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name mind-dev.eatonfamily.net;

    # Relaxed caching for development
    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data:; connect-src 'self';" always;

    # Static files from dev deployment
    location / {
        root /usr/share/nginx/html/mind-dev;
        try_files $uri $uri/ /index.html;
        
        # Minimal caching for development
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|woff|woff2)$ {
            expires 5m;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        # No caching for HTML files in dev
        location = /index.html {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # Same PocketBase API (shared backend)
    location /api/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
        proxy_http_version 1.1;
        proxy_set_header Upgrade $http_upgrade;
        proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
    }

    # PocketBase Admin
    location /_/ {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/_/;
        proxy_set_header Host $host;
        proxy_set_header X-Real-IP $remote_addr;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For $proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
        proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto $scheme;
    }

    # Health check
    location /health {
        proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/health;
        access_log off;
    }
}
```

## Migration Steps

### Step 1: Setup Directory Structure

```bash
# Create main directories
mkdir -p /volume1/docker/{nginx,pocketbase}

# Create nginx subdirectories
mkdir -p /volume1/docker/nginx/{configs/sites-available,configs/ssl,scripts}

# Create pocketbase subdirectories  
mkdir -p /volume1/docker/pocketbase/{data/{pb_data,pb_public,pb_migrations},scripts}

# Set proper ownership for pocketbase data
chown -R 1028:100 /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/
```

### Step 2: Deploy Configuration Files

```bash
# Copy all the config files shown above to their respective locations
# nginx.conf -> /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/nginx.conf
# site configs -> /volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/
```

### Step 3: Deploy Single Stack in Portainer

1. **Deploy the combined stack:**
   - Go to Stacks in Portainer
   - Create new stack: `web-apps`
   - Paste the updated compose content (includes both nginx and pocketbase)
   - Deploy

### Step 4: Test New Setup

- Visit `http://mind.eatonfamily.net` (should work via your reverse proxy)
- Visit `http://calcium.eatonfamily.net`  
- Visit `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-dev/`
- Visit `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/calcium-dev/`
- Check PocketBase admin: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-dev/_/`

### Step 5: Migrate PocketBase Data (After Testing)

Once the new containers are working:
```bash
# Stop the new stack temporarily
# Copy data from old location to new
cp -r /volume1/projects/mind-pwa/pocketbase/pb_data/* /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_data/
cp -r /volume1/projects/mind-pwa/pocketbase/pb_public/* /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_public/
cp -r /volume1/projects/mind-pwa/pocketbase/pb_migrations/* /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/pb_migrations/

# Fix ownership
chown -R 1028:100 /volume1/docker/pocketbase/data/

# Restart stack in Portainer
```

## Management Scripts

### Environment-Aware Nginx Reload Script

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/scripts/reload-config.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash
echo "🔄 Testing nginx configuration..."
if docker exec nginx-proxy nginx -t; then
    echo "✅ Configuration is valid, reloading..."
    docker exec nginx-proxy nginx -s reload
    echo "✅ Configuration reloaded successfully"
    echo ""
    echo "🌐 Available endpoints:"
    echo "  Production:"
    echo "    - https://mind.eatonfamily.net"
    echo "    - https://calcium.eatonfamily.net"
    echo "  Development (Local):"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/Ca-pwa-dev/"
    echo "    - http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/_/ (PocketBase Admin)"
else
    echo "❌ Configuration test failed! Not reloading."
    exit 1
fi
```

### Utility Scripts - When and How to Use

The migration plan includes several utility scripts. Here's when you'd use each:

#### **1. `reload-config.sh` - Most Common**
**When to use:**
- After making changes to nginx configuration files
- After adding new sites or modifying existing ones
- When troubleshooting nginx issues

**How to use:**
```bash
cd /volume1/docker/nginx/scripts
./reload-config.sh
```

**Why it's useful:**
- Tests configuration before applying (prevents breaking nginx)
- Shows you all available endpoints after reload
- Safer than restarting the entire container

#### **2. `add-site.sh` - When Adding New Apps**
**When to use:**
- Adding a brand new web application
- Setting up staging environments for existing apps

**How to use:**
```bash
cd /volume1/docker/nginx/scripts
./add-site.sh myapp myapp.eatonfamily.net
```

**What it does:**
- Creates nginx config template for new app
- Tells you what volume mount to add in Portainer
- Provides both static and PocketBase-enabled templates

#### **3. PocketBase Scripts (Future)**
These would be useful for data management:

**`/volume1/docker/pocketbase/scripts/backup.sh`** - Database backups
**`/volume1/docker/pocketbase/scripts/restore.sh`** - Database restoration

### Script Usage Frequency

**Daily Development:**
- Your existing deployment scripts: `./deploy.sh dev/prod`
- No utility scripts needed

**Weekly/Monthly:**
- `reload-config.sh` - When adding features or new apps
- Your scripts handle 99% of routine work

**Rarely (New Apps):**
- `add-site.sh` - Only when adding completely new applications
- Backup/restore scripts - Only for major changes or migrations

### Your Scripts Are Excellent

Your deployment scripts are actually **better** than the utility scripts for routine work because they:
- ✅ Handle the full build-deploy cycle
- ✅ Support multiple environments seamlessly  
- ✅ Include error handling and validation
- ✅ Show build sizes and helpful output
- ✅ Are specific to your app needs

The utility scripts are more for **infrastructure changes** rather than **application deployments**.

## Benefits of This Architecture

### Add New Site Template

**File:** `/volume1/docker/nginx/scripts/add-site.sh`

```bash
#!/bin/bash
SITE_NAME=$1
DOMAIN=$2

if [ -z "$SITE_NAME" ] || [ -z "$DOMAIN" ]; then
    echo "Usage: $0 <site-name> <domain>"
    echo "Example: $0 todoapp todo.eatonfamily.net"
    exit 1
fi

cat > "/volume1/docker/nginx/configs/sites-available/${DOMAIN}.conf" << EOF
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name ${DOMAIN};

    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data:;" always;

    location / {
        root /usr/share/nginx/html/${SITE_NAME};
        try_files \$uri \$uri/ /index.html;
        
        location ~* \.(js|css|png|jpg|jpeg|gif|ico|svg|woff|woff2)\$ {
            expires 1y;
            add_header Cache-Control "public, no-transform";
        }
        
        location = /index.html {
            add_header Cache-Control "no-cache, no-store, must-revalidate";
        }
    }

    # Uncomment if app needs PocketBase backend:
    # location /api/ {
    #     proxy_pass http://pocketbase_backend/api/;
    #     proxy_set_header Host \$host;
    #     proxy_set_header X-Real-IP \$remote_addr;
    #     proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-For \$proxy_add_x_forwarded_for;
    #     proxy_set_header X-Forwarded-Proto \$scheme;
    #     proxy_http_version 1.1;
    #     proxy_set_header Upgrade \$http_upgrade;
    #     proxy_set_header Connection "upgrade";
    # }
}
EOF

echo "✅ Created config for ${DOMAIN}"
echo "📝 Remember to:"
echo "   1. Add volume mount in Portainer: /volume1/web/${SITE_NAME}-deploy:/usr/share/nginx/html/${SITE_NAME}:ro"
echo "   2. Restart nginx-proxy stack"
```

## Additional Considerations for Dev/Prod Setup

### Local Development URLs
With this configuration, your development URLs will be (matching your current setup):
- **MIND Diet Tracker Dev**: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/`
- **Calcium Tracker Dev**: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/Ca-pwa-dev/`
- **PocketBase Admin**: `http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/_/`

### Your Deployment Scripts Work Perfectly!

Looking at your deployment scripts, they're excellent and **no changes needed**:

✅ **MIND App Scripts:**
- `./deploy-client.sh dev` → deploys to `/volume1/web/mind-pwa-dev`
- `./deploy-pocketbase.sh dev` → deploys to `/volume1/web/mind-pwa-dev` 

✅ **Calcium App Script:**
- `./deploy.sh dev` → deploys to `/volume1/web/Ca-pwa-dev`
- `./deploy.sh prod` → deploys to `/volume1/web/Ca-pwa-deploy`

### Development Workflow (No Changes Required)
```bash
# Deploy MIND app for development
cd /volume1/projects/mind-pwa
./deploy-pocketbase.sh dev
# Visit: http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/mind-pwa-dev/

# Deploy Calcium app for development  
cd /volume1/projects/Ca-pwa
./deploy.sh dev
# Visit: http://eatonmediasvr.local:8080/Ca-pwa-dev/

# Deploy to production when ready
./deploy-pocketbase.sh prod  # MIND
./deploy.sh prod            # Calcium
```

1. **Modular**: Nginx and PocketBase are separate, manageable stacks
2. **Scalable**: Easy to add new apps without complex reconfigurations  
3. **Maintainable**: All configurations are version-controlled and organized
4. **Flexible**: Apps can use PocketBase or be purely static
5. **Production Ready**: Proper security, caching, and health checks
6. **Portainer Friendly**: Managed through familiar UI with proper dependency handling

## Future Expansion

When you add new apps:
1. Deploy app static files to `/volume1/web/newapp-deploy`
2. Run `add-site.sh newapp newapp.eatonfamily.net`
3. Update nginx-proxy stack to include new volume mount
4. Apps automatically get shared PocketBase access if needed

This setup gives you a robust foundation for your development work while being production-ready!

<file path="configs/sites-available/calcium-dev.eatonfamily.net.conf">
# Development/Staging environment for Calcium Tracker
server {
    listen 80;
    server_name calcium-dev.eatonfamily.net;

    # Security header remains the same
    add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; connect-src 'self' https://*.workers.dev https://api.ocr.space https://api.nal.usda.gov https://world.openfoodfacts.org; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' fonts.googleapis.com; font-src 'self' fonts.gstatic.com; img-src 'self' data: blob:;" always;

    # --- THIS IS THE CRITICAL FIX ---
    # We now match the specific sub-path that your dev build uses.
    location /Ca-pwa-dev/ {
        # 'alias' maps the URL path directly to the filesystem path.
        # It replaces the '/Ca-pwa-dev/' part of the URL with this path.
        alias /usr/share/nginx/html/Ca-pwa-dev/;

        # The SPA fallback rule now correctly points to the index.html inside the sub-path.
        try_files $uri $uri/ /Ca-pwa-dev/index.html;
    }

    # This is a user-friendly redirect. If someone goes to the root of the domain,
    # it sends them to the correct application path.
    location = / {
        return 302 /Ca-pwa-dev/;
    }
}
</file>
